MODULE 55: AI DEVELOPMENT AGENT PROTOCOLS, CONTEXT INJECTION PIPELINES & CODE-GENERATION GUARDRAILS
To execute the technical implementation of Folk-Idle using an AI coding agent (e.g., Claude, GPT-4o, or Gemini) without experiencing context drift, code fragmentation, or architectural degradation, the agent must be bound by a strict set of rules. This module establishes the exact system configuration prompts, ingestion sequence, and code guardrails required to guide the AI through the development process.
1. The Core Architectural Commandments for the AI Agent
Any AI agent assigned to generate code for Folk-Idle must have these four rules permanently pinned to its active memory context:
+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+|                            AI CODER SYSTEM COMMANDMENTS                           |+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+|  1. SERVER IS TRUTH : Client-side scripts are strictly predictive visualization   ||                       proxies. No logic updates state locally.                    ||                                                                                   ||  2. ZERO ALLOCATION : 10 Hz simulation components MUST use C# unmanaged memory    ||                       (NativeArray, structs) and bypass the Unity GC.            ||                                                                                   ||  3. SERIALIZABLE DB : All database operations involving currency or item trading ||                       MUST use strict Serializable Isolation row locks.           ||                                                                                   ||  4. NO PLAIN TEXT   : Code templates must exclude plain text secrets, string API  ||                       paths, or exposed metadata endpoints.                       |+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
2. Context Ingestion Protocol (Preventing Hallucinations)
Do not feed all 55 modules into the AI agent simultaneously. This saturates the attention heads, leading to lazy code generation, truncated scripts, and forgotten edge-case handlers. The implementation must follow a staged, token-conserving injection pipeline aligned with the MVP roadmap.
The Ingestion Sequence Matrix
[Phase 1: Database & Memory Layout] ---> Inject Modules 40, 48, 51, 54                                          Result: Core Data Models & Schema                                               |                                               v[Phase 2: Clock & Simulation Engine] ---> Inject Modules 10, 42, 44, 46                                          Result: 10 Hz Tick Engine & Time Banks                                               |                                               v[Phase 3: Visual & Sync Mesh]       ---> Inject Modules 45, 47, 53                                          Result: Forge & Predictive LERP
3. Production-Grade System Prompt Blueprint
Copy and paste the markdown payload below into the AI Agent’s System Prompt or initial initialization prompt before starting any coding task.
Role: Senior Backend & Systems Engineer specializing in High-Concurrency Architecture, Unity IL2CPP optimization, and distributed PostgreSQL/Redis environments.Task: Implement codebase components for the Folk-Idle platform based on specified design modules.Strict Technical Constraints for Code Generation:1. C# Memory Allocation:   - Inside the 10 Hz simulation loop, never allocate memory to the managed heap. No LINQ operations, no local instantiations of classes, and no lambda expressions that trigger closures.   - Use structs passed by reference ('in', 'out', 'ref') and 'NativeArray' layouts using unmanaged memory boundaries.2. Relational Database Operations (PostgreSQL):   - All state modifications (Gold modifications, market execution, item fusions, salvage operations) must run inside explicit transactions utilizing the Serializable isolation level.   - You must append explicit 'FOR UPDATE' row-locking commands to all entity selection loops to prevent multi-threaded duplication exploits.3. String and Security Protection:   - Never embed explicit string literals for API paths or credentials into code blocks.   - Compile code templates utilizing configuration wrappers or encrypted byte structures ready for IL2CPP stripping.4. Error Handling:   - Every single database transaction block must wrap within a Try/Catch structure that forces an explicit, complete rollback upon failure. Never leave a transaction dangling or uncommitted.   - Return clean typed operational results ('Enum') instead of generic boolean true/false flags.Workflow Protocol:- Implement step-by-step. Do not provide truncated loops, placeholders, or '// TODO' comments.- Generate production-ready, highly optimized code blocks with complete variable typing.- If a target structural dependency from a prior module is missing, ask for its schema boundary definition before generating code.
4. Execution Guardrail Verification Loop
Before accepting any code block generated by the AI agent, cross-reference its output against this operational verification checklist. If any of these checks fail, reject the code block and order the agent to re-run the calculation loop.
                  +-----------------------------------------+                  |     AI Agent Generates Source Code      |                  +-----------------------------------------+                                       |                                       v                  +-----------------------------------------+                  |  Check A: Does it use Managed Heap?     |---> [YES] -> REJECT & RE-PROMPT                  +-----------------------------------------+                                       | [NO]                                       v                  +-----------------------------------------+                  |  Check B: Are DB row locks pessimistic? |---> [NO]  -> REJECT & RE-PROMPT                  +-----------------------------------------+                                       | [YES]                                       v                  +-----------------------------------------+                  |  Check C: Are there placeholders/TODOs? |---> [YES] -> REJECT & RE-PROMPT                  +-----------------------------------------+                                       | [NO]                                       v                  +-----------------------------------------+                  |       Accept Code Into MVP Branch       |                  +-----------------------------------------+
This protocol guarantees that the AI coding agent remains constrained by the security, optimization, and balance decisions established across the entire 54-module blueprint, shielding the MVP architecture from code degradation.

MODULE 54: POST-MIGRATION INTEGRATION AUDIT, EDGE-CASE ANOMALIES & LIVE BUG FIX REGISTRY
This module serves as a centralized registry for structural errors, logical contradictions, and architectural vulnerabilities identified during the transition from the durability model to the durability-free Forge model. All future fixes, patches, and edge-case remediations will be formally tracked in this document under unique BUG-FIX tickets.
1. Active Anomaly Registry (Identified System Flaws)
BUG-FIX-01: Durability Legacy Compile Exception
Source Module: Module 53 (Sections 1.2 and 3)
Classification: Fatal (Causes compilation failure)
Description: The C# code inside ForgeSplicingEngine contains legacy references to MaximumDurability and CurrentDurability properties, which were completely removed from the database schema in Module 51. Attempting to compile triggers a Cs0117: 'MarketEquipmentInstance' does not contain a definition for 'MaximumDurability'.
BUG-FIX-02: Identity Typology Exploitation (Trash-Spam Vector)
Source Module: Module 53 (Section 1.1)
Classification: High (Economic exploit)
Description: The term "identical item" for fusion was not clearly bounded within the data model. If the system required matching randomized affixes, fusion would be mathematically impossible. If it only requires a matching item_base_id, elite players will buy up the cheapest T1 trash on the market to use as cheap upgrade fuel for their high-end, "god-roll" primary weapons, destroying the premium market value of well-crafted gear.
BUG-FIX-03: Guild Liquidity Stagnation (MVP Deadlock)
Source Module: Module 51 (Section 3) & Module 48
Classification: Medium (Deflationary trap)
Description: The settlement engine skims a tax from every transaction and stores it in the guild's vault_gold_balance. Because mechanics like Guild Wars are pushed to later post-MVP phases, guild vaults act as a one-way black hole for liquidity. This causes circulating currency to freeze, triggering artificial market deflation within the first 14 days of launch.
BUG-FIX-04: Seasonal Archive Transaction WAL Bloat
Source Module: Module 51 (Section 2)
Classification: High (Infrastructure collapse)
Description: Executing a massive INSERT INTO historical_market_archives SELECT ... FROM market_order_ledger command block across millions of rows at the exact moment of the seasonal reset locks the Write-Ahead Log (WAL) and causes API gateway timeouts, crashing the database cluster.
2. Resolution Patches & Refactored Source Components
The following corrective patches rewrite the faulty behaviors of the preceding modules.
Patch for BUG-FIX-01 & BUG-FIX-02 (Refactored Forge Engine)
This patch removes durability variables and modifies the fusion penalty rules. For Tier 2 items, failure now applies a permanent lock to a random affix slot (is_affix_locked) instead of degrading durability.
// Rewriting the failure block inside ExecuteItemFusionAsync (Module 53)if (roll > successProbability){    // Evict sacrificial records from persistence memory    dbContext.EquipmentInstances.Remove(sac1);    dbContext.EquipmentInstances.Remove(sac2);    if (currentTier >= 3)    {        // High-Tier Penalty: Vaporize the primary item row completely        dbContext.EquipmentInstances.Remove(primaryItem);        await dbContext.SaveChangesAsync();        await transaction.CommitAsync();        return ForgeResult.CreateCriticalFailure("CRITICAL_FAILURE_ALL_DESTROYED");    }    // Correction for BUG-FIX-01: Durability-free penalty for Tier 2 failure    // Modifies JSONB metadata payload to permanently lock a random affix against future re-rolls    primaryItem.AffixDataPayload = EnforceAffixLockoutPenalty(primaryItem.AffixDataPayload);        await dbContext.SaveChangesAsync();    await transaction.CommitAsync();    return ForgeResult.CreatePartialFailure(primaryItem.InstanceId, "SACRIFICIAL_DESTROYED_PRIMARY_AFFIX_LOCKED");}
Patch for BUG-FIX-02 (Material Fusion Index)
To ensure high-quality crafts maintain an appropriate market value floor compared to trash drops, the fusion gold cost (C_{\text{fusion}}) scales based on the quality tiers of the sacrificial items:
C_{\text{fusion}} = C_{\text{base\_tier}} \times \left( 1 + \sum_{i=1}^{2} (4 - \text{SacrificeQuality}_i) \times 0.50 \right)
If a player uses the worst quality tier (Quality = 1) fodder to upgrade an Excellent item, they pay 300\% more in gold transaction fees than if they used matching quality equivalents. This flattens the systemic exploit vector by equalizing raw trading parameters.
Patch for BUG-FIX-03 (MVP Liquidity Burn Redirect)
Until full guild expenditure features are deployed, the guild transaction tax within the GlobalMarketSettlementEngine is routed away from the guild treasury and burned directly.
// Correction for BUG-FIX-03: Redirecting guild tax during MVP phase// Instead of storing gold within the guild vault, the currency is instantly burned to counter inflationint guildCut = (int)(grossTransactionCost * (order.GuildTaxRateApplied / 100.0));int marketSinkBurn = (int)(grossTransactionCost * 0.03);// MVP Emergency Patch: 100% of the guild cut is added to the system sink burnint totalGoldBurned = guildCut + marketSinkBurn; buyerBalance.CurrentGold -= grossTransactionCost;if (sellerBalance != null) sellerBalance.CurrentGold += (grossTransactionCost - totalGoldBurned);// guildVault.VaultGoldBalance += guildCut; <-- DISENGAGED FOR MVP LIFECYCLE STAGE
Patch for BUG-FIX-04 (Continuous Ledger Archiving)
The large, single-batch INSERT ... SELECT operation is purged from the seasonal reset loop. Completed orders are written to the historical archive asynchronously at the exact millisecond of order matching within the GlobalMarketSettlementEngine. The seasonal reset sequence now processes a rapid TRUNCATE command over empty or near-empty active tables.
-- Replacement for step 4 in the seasonal market reset routine (Module 51.2)-- Table contains only unfulfilled/cancelled late-season orders. History processing is now fully active on-the-fly.TRUNCATE TABLE market_order_ledger RESTART IDENTITY CASCADE;

SYSTEM AMENDMENT: ELIMINATION OF TOOL DURABILITY MECHANICS
Removing durability aligns perfectly with core idle game design principles. It eliminates a major user experience bottleneck—where offline progression is prematurely cut off due to a broken pickaxe—and significantly reduces server database write overhead.
Here is the re-engineered architectural specification for the permanent tool progression system.
1. Database Optimization & Asynchronous Scalability
Transition to O(1) Offline Processing: The offline engine no longer needs to run step-by-step chronological loop simulations to check the exact timestamp a tool breaks. Reward generation becomes a pure, deterministic mathematical function: \text{Resources Earned} = \lfloor \frac{T_{\text{eff}}}{\text{Base Action Time} \times (1 - \text{Speed Modifier}\%)} \rfloor \times \text{Yield Multiplier}
Database Write Reduction: Removes constant database transaction mutations updating durability counters on every single extraction tick. Tools are stripped of individual item instance data rows and are instead stored as a flat global integer index (current_tool_tier) inside the village registry table.
2. Replenishing the Gold Sink Economy
To prevent macroeconomic hyperinflation caused by removing continuous tool repair costs, the economic drainage is shifted directly into progression gating:
Radical Upgrade Cost Scaling: The flat Gold and Refined Bar costs to unlock sequential tool tiers are increased by 150% to 200% to compensate for the lifetime lack of maintenance fees.
Operational Refining Taxes: Manufacturing tasks (Smelting, Cooking, Alchemy) now enforce a minor, flat transactional Gold fee per batched production queue initialization.
3. Global Permanent Tool Progression Matrix
Tools now exist as permanent, account-wide infrastructural upgrades unlocked via the Village Workshop interface.

MODULE 42: OFFLINE TIME BANKING, CHRONO-ACCELERATION MECHANICS & TIME DISTORTION PIPELINES
1. The Chrono-Buffer Time Banking Framework
To maximize player retention during periods of extended absence and monetize engagement through catch-up loops, Folk-Idle implements a server-authoritative Chrono-Buffer Time Banking System. When a player remains offline past the 24-hour efficiency degradation limits, or when they acquire premium "Chrono-Cap" items, excess time is converted into a secondary account resource: banked_chrono_seconds.
1.1 Chrono-Buffer Accumulation Curve
Offline time passing beyond the primary efficiency threshold (T_{\text{threshold}} = 86,400\text{ seconds}) is captured and routed into the banked reservoir at a diminishing efficiency rate governed by a logarithmic decay function:
\Delta S_{\text{banked}} = \max \left( 0, \lfloor \ln(T_{\text{offline}} - T_{\text{threshold}} + 1) \times \psi \rfloor \right)
Where:
T_{\text{offline}} is the total raw elapsed offline duration in seconds.
\psi is the system-defined conversion scaling constant, hard-locked via Remote Config at exactly 1200.0.
The maximum storage volume for banked_chrono_seconds is rigidly capped at 604,800\text{ seconds} (7 Calendar Days) to prevent permanent simulation distortion.
1.2 Resource Expenditure & Action Loop Acceleration
Players execute banked time through the client interface to supercharge active processing slots. Activating Chrono-Acceleration forces the server's tick engine to process the targeted action loop at an accelerated rate (2\times or 4\times speed scaling factor).
For every real-world second elapsed (t_{\text{real}}) while acceleration is active, the engine consumes a corresponding deduction block from the banked reservoir:
\text{Buffer Drain} = t_{\text{real}} \times (M_{\text{speed}} - 1)
Where M_{\text{speed}} represents the active speed multiplier coefficient (M_{\text{speed}} \in \{2.0, 4.0\}).
2. Server-Authoritative Instantaneous Time Warp Resolution Loop
In addition to dynamic multi-speed throttling, players can consume discrete items (e.g., "2-Hour Fast Forward Core") to instantly resolve production queues. To prevent thread lockouts across thousands of concurrent slot simulations, the server processes these instant injections using a pure deterministic mathematical jump rather than stepping through sequential tick-frames.
2.1 Instant Time Warp Execution Routine (C# Backend Assembly)
public class TimeWarpProcessingEngine{    public WarpResolutionResult ResolveInstantWarp(CharacterSimulationState characterState, int warpDurationSeconds)    {        int totalRemainingWarpSeconds = warpDurationSeconds;        int completedActionLoopsCount = 0;        int totalAccumulatedXpReward = 0;                // Read immutable core timing parameters directly from the engine reference        int baseActionCycleTime = characterState.ActiveNode.BaseActionTimeSeconds;        double speedModifierCoefficient = characterState.DerivedStats.GlobalSpeedModifier;         int netActionCycleTime = (int)Math.Max(1, Math.Round(baseActionCycleTime * (1.0 - speedModifierCoefficient)));        // Execute deterministic chunk division loop        if (netActionCycleTime <= totalRemainingWarpSeconds)        {            completedActionLoopsCount = totalRemainingWarpSeconds / netActionCycleTime;            totalRemainingWarpSeconds %= netActionCycleTime;                        totalAccumulatedXpReward = completedActionLoopsCount * characterState.ActiveNode.BaseXpReward;        }        return new WarpResolutionResult        {            CalculatedLoopExecutions = completedActionLoopsCount,            InjectedXpVolume = totalAccumulatedXpReward,            UnusedUnprocessedSeconds = totalRemainingWarpSeconds,            ExecutionTimestamp = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow.ToUnixTimeSeconds()        };    }}
3. Database Storage & Concurrency Safeguards for Time Injections
Time manipulation vectors are highly vulnerable targets for concurrency attacks, such as double-spending speed items via latency injection or modifying client device clocks. Folk-Idle prevents these exploits by making the server clock the sole authority for all calculations.
3.1 Account Chrono-Registry Data Schema
CREATE TABLE account_chrono_registry (    account_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,    banked_chrono_seconds INT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,    active_speed_multiplier NUMERIC(3,1) DEFAULT 1.0 NOT NULL,    acceleration_termination_epoch BIGINT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,    last_clock_sync_epoch BIGINT NOT NULL,    CONSTRAINT chk_chrono_bounds CHECK (banked_chrono_seconds BETWEEN 0 AND 604800),    CONSTRAINT chk_multiplier_values CHECK (active_speed_multiplier IN (1.0, 2.0, 4.0)));
3.2 Anti-Exploit Atomic Verification Transaction
When a client requests a Time Warp consumption or toggles an active speed modification state, the server applies a rigid pessimistic row lock (SELECT FOR UPDATE) on the targeted profile. This forces all concurrent requests to queue sequentially, neutralizing double-minting exploits at the database boundary.
BEGIN;-- Step 1: Secure an absolute row-level lock on the profile's chrono registry parametersSELECT banked_chrono_seconds, last_clock_sync_epochFROM account_chrono_registryWHERE account_id = '9b1deb4d-3b7d-4bad-9bdd-2b0d7b3dcb6d'FOR UPDATE;-- Step 2: Validate the client context using true server NTP timestamps, rejecting local device modificationsUPDATE account_chrono_registrySET banked_chrono_seconds = banked_chrono_seconds - 3600,    active_speed_multiplier = 2.0,    acceleration_termination_epoch = (EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM NOW()) + 3600)::BIGINT,    last_clock_sync_epoch = (EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM NOW()))::BIGINTWHERE account_id = '9b1deb4d-3b7d-4bad-9bdd-2b0d7b3dcb6d'  AND banked_chrono_seconds >= 3600;COMMIT;
If the transaction fails to acquire the lock or determines that the banked_chrono_seconds parameter drops below the validation constraints, the entire operation is rolled back, and an anomaly alert packet is routed straight to the player monitoring infrastructure (Module 25).

MODULE 19: SOUND DESIGN, VISUAL ART DIRECTION & ASSET PRODUCTION PIPELINES
1. Acoustic Architecture & Dynamic Audio States
To align with the ancient and medieval European folklore themes, the soundscape relies heavily on period-authentic acoustic instruments, avoiding synthesized elements. The audio engine operates asynchronously, decoupling sound layer triggers from the core game state simulation ticks to protect processing threads on low-end mobile devices.
1.1 Instrumentation Profiles
Slavic/Bohemian Zones (Regions 01, 05): Dominant use of the husle (folk fiddle), kobza, wood flutes, and basic frame drums.
Celtic/Highland Zones (Regions 02, 06): Dominant use of bagpipes, tin whistles, bodhrán drums, and acoustic harps.
Germanic/Alpine Zones (Regions 03, 04, 07): Dominant use of alpine horns, dulcimers, hurdy-gurdies, and heavy metallic anvil impacts for subterranean environments.
Norse/Northern Zones (Regions 09, 10): Dominant use of tagelharpa, bukkehorn, deep throat chanting layers, and heavy low-frequency skin drums.
1.2 Dynamic Music State Machine
The global Audio Mixer switches background music tracks dynamically based on the active slots’ allocation states via a smooth 2.0-second cross-fade matrix.
State - Village Management: Light, rhythmic string arrangements with ambient bird calls and crackling forge fires, optimizing a calm, mathematical pacing environment.
State - Standard Gathering: Repetitive, steady tempo percussion loops syncopated with individual asset impact cues (e.g., wood ax thuds or pickaxe strikes on solid stone) to reinforce action loops.
State - Region Combat Grinding: Aggressive, mid-tempo percussion arrangements with rising string sections. The tempo scales upward by exactly 15% when an account shifts its active focus to an Elite monster node.
State - Regional Boss Encounter: Fast, high-stakes orchestral compositions featuring authentic folk elements mixed with deep choral arrangements. Boss audio themes run on a high-priority mixer bus, overriding secondary ambient sounds.
2. Visual Art Style & Graphic User Interface (GUI) Guidelines
Folk-Idle utilizes a data-dense, dark grim-fantasy visual presentation modeled directly on medieval European woodcut illustrations, parchment textures, and desaturated watercolor aesthetics. This minimizes GPU rendering overhead, shifting processing focus to background math matrices.
2.1 Interface Color Palette Blueprint
The interface utilizes an strict six-color hexadecimal schema to ensure typography readability against textured parchment canvas backgrounds.
Primary Parchment Background: #F2EBD9 (Desaturated warm beige)
Deep Text/Shadow Lining: #1A1612 (Near-black charcoal brown)
Active Accent Trim: #8C251C (Muted crimson oxblood red)
Secondary Informational Text: #4A443A (Muted grayish-brown)
Premium Currency Indicator: #1E6B7B (Deep Baltic sea teal)
Inactive Component State: #A69E8F (Desaturated ash gray)
2.2 UI Typography Rules
The game architecture limits asset deployment to exactly two font families to preserve memory spaces during runtime rendering.
Header Typography (Titles, Region Names, Level Milestones): Medieval gothic calligraphy font types (e.g., clean Blackletter or Uncial derivatives). Hard restriction: Limited to non-interactive decorative label headings only.
Operational Data Typography (Stats, Quantities, Chat logs, Timers): High-legibility serif text configurations (e.g., Garamond or Crimson Text style matrices). Hard restriction: Must maintain clear character definitions down to an 8-point sizing matrix on mobile displays.
3. UI Motion & Juice Optimization Mechanics
Because Folk-Idle is a menu-driven title lacking complex 3D environments, the player's sense of gameplay weight depends entirely on crisp, lightweight UI micro-interactions (juice) that cause zero battery or CPU degradation.
3.1 Non-GPU Vector Easing Loops
Button toggles, navigation pane transitions, and panel expanders utilize simple mathematical interpolation curves (Ease-Out-Cubic matrices) executed entirely within pure C# logic frameworks, bypassing complex structural Unity animation component layers.
Hover/Press States: Selected panels shift size by a flat factor of 1.05x while shifting their background hue toward the Active Accent color over exactly 0.08 seconds.
Tab Swapping: Sliding panel frames enter view spaces laterally, transitioning across a flat 150-pixel buffer over exactly 0.12 seconds before finalizing text data updates.
3.2 Action Ticker Particle Spawning Restrictions
To prevent multi-character active combat calculations from overwhelming particle processing pools during fast attack speed cycles:
Damage Text Overlays: Numbers spawn at randomized coordinate offsets within a tight 40-pixel bounding box centered on the monster portrait.
Movement Profiles: Numbers accelerate vertically upwards by 80 pixels over 0.40 seconds before fading alpha values smoothly to zero.
Capping Rules: A maximum of 6 concurrent damage numbers can exist in the active combat view hierarchy at any given timestamp. Subsequent hits combine aditivelty if they happen within a single 0.1-second tick window.
4. Visual Asset Naming Conventions & Sprite Sheet Layouts
To streamline automated build processes inside the Unity engine, all graphics must strictly follow a hard-coded namespace hierarchy.
4.1 Asset Folder Namespace Syntax
Assets must use lower-case characters separated by singular underscores, categorized by their systemic target function.
Syntax Structure: spr_ui_panel_type_index
Example 01: spr_ui_button_navigation_active_01
Example 02: spr_ico_item_copper_sword_t01
Example 03: spr_por_race_draugr_old_male
4.2 Sprite Sheet Packing Limits
Individual item symbols, professional tool graphics, and resource node illustrations are grouped into unified texture atlas blocks to optimize GPU draw calls.
Atlas Resolution Target: 2048 x 2048 pixels maximum per atlas category, utilizing compressed 8-bit texture sheets.
Padding Grid Restraints: Every individual item graphic is designed as a square 128 x 128 pixel sprite matrix, isolated by a hard 2-pixel transparent padding perimeter buffer to completely eliminate graphical edge bleeding during canvas scaling operations on extreme mobile aspect ratios.
MODULE 20: LOCALIZATION, ACCESSIBILITY COMPLIANCE & MASTER INTEGRATION MATRIX
1. Internationalization (i18n) & Localized Schema Keyboards
Folk-Idle isolates all user-facing interface text strings from core execution components by implementing a relational dictionary key tracking index system. Text keys point to localized flat string sheets loaded into application cache tables at boot.
1.1 Core Localization Language Registry
The game natively packs string databases covering four primary geographic regions associated with the historical origins of the folklore assets.
Language Index 01: English (en-US) - Universal Default Baseline Schema
Language Index 02: Czech (cs-CZ) - Primary Folklore Operational Regional Key
Language Index 03: German (de-DE) - Central European Folklore Focus Layer
Language Index 04: Polish (pl-PL) - West-Slavic Folklore Language Extension
1.2 Multi-Language Structural Schema Template
The string table uses a flat key-value architecture to preserve system memory space and ensure instant text layout updates during runtime.
Key: ui_lbl_population_count | English: "Population: {0} / {1} Citizens" | Czech: "Populace: {0} / {1} Obyvatel" | German: "Bevölkerung: {0} / {1} Bürger" | Polish: "Populacja: {0} / {1} Mieszkańców"
Key: ui_lbl_combat_hit_log | English: "{0} strikes {1} for {2} damage." | Czech: "{0} útočí na {1} za {2} poškození." | German: "{0} trifft {1} für {2} Schaden." | Polish: "{0} atakuje {1} zadając {2} obrażeń."
Key: ui_lbl_forge_error_gold | English: "Insufficient Gold for item upgrade." | Czech: "Nedostatek zlata pro vylepšení předmětu." | German: "Unzureichendes Gold für Gegenstands-Upgrade." | Polish: "Niewystarczająca ilość złota do ulepszenia przedmiotu."
2. Accessibility (a11y) Screen Overlay Core Controls
To ensure accessibility compliance across global application marketplaces without altering the data-heavy design aesthetic, the game engine incorporates a specialized Accessibility Options Manager.
2.1 Dynamic Colorblind Adaptation Filters
Because item rarities (Tiers 1 to 14) and interface warnings rely heavily on color-coded designations, the UI pipeline processes all text colors through an adaptation shader block when a colorblind filter state is toggled active.
Protanopia/Deuteranopia Mode: Shifts red and green accent components toward high-contrast blue and yellow color spaces. Rarity borders automatically append a text-based tier prefix tag (e.g., "[T7] Legendary Sword" instead of relying solely on a gold color trim line).
Tritanopia Mode: Adjusts light blue and teal components into stark desaturated white and deep charcoal shades to preserve reading clarity.
2.2 Text Scaling and Screen-Reader Integration Hooks
Dynamic Font Padding: Users can scale the sizing parameters of the serif typography elements by up to 135% through the settings panel. Interface text containers are designed with adaptive vertical expansion margins to completely prevent word wrapping conflicts or layout clipping during scaling operations.
Haptic Heartbeat Indicators: For silent or visually impaired play settings, mobile devices execute tiny haptic motor impulses matching combat cycle outcomes (e.g., a faint 10-millisecond vibration for a successful hit, a sharp double-pulse for an emergency Auto-Eat food trigger execution).
3. Data Protection, GDPR Compliance & Privacy Infrastructures
Because Folk-Idle uses cloud synchronization tracking profiles, leaderboard databases, and online guild interaction registries, the backend architecture must adhere strictly to international data privacy frameworks (including EU-GDPR and California Consumer Privacy Act directives).
3.1 Strict Player Profile Sanitization Protocols
PII Isolation Safeguards: The characters, items, and character_skills database tables defined in Module 01 contain zero personally identifiable information (PII). Accounts are linked exclusively to an anonymous, server-generated user UUID token issued by the Supabase/Firebase authentication provider framework.
Analytics Tracking Restrictions: IP addresses, geolocations, and telemetry parameters are completely anonymized before transmission to background analytic logging modules, preventing tracking links to individual accounts.
3.2 Automated Account Purging (The Right to be Forgotten)
The Settings interface features an explicit, irreversible "Delete Village Infrastructure Data" terminal button pathway.
Deletion Pipeline: Activating this command prompts a safety confirmation window. Upon confirmation, the client transmits an authenticated purge request to the server API node.
Database Execution Action: The server executes a cascading deletion query row sweep based on the user's secret ID token. This drops all rows inside the characters, items, character_equipment, and village infrastructure state entries instantly. Any active guild memberships drop immediately, removing historical log instances and permanently clearing the account profile from global ladder lists within 60 seconds.
4. Master GDD Integration Verification Checklist
This final sign-off checklist serves as the absolute verification criteria for the engineering team prior to initiating active production builds across the Unity frontend environment and the PostgreSQL backend servers.
4.1 Architecture and Math Verification Passes
Verify that the 3-slot asynchronous FSM tracking controllers correctly calculate individual profession loops without creating database transaction collisions.
Confirm that the 4-tier offline time degradation logic correctly cuts off resource extraction loops the exact moment tool durability metrics strike zero.
Validate that the 14-tier geometric forge formula requires exactly 1,594,323 Normal item bases to synthesize one clean Transcendent tier end-game equipment piece.
4.2 LiveOps & Security Validation Checks
Assert that the server-side NTP verification engine drops and rolls back any client state update payload displaying local system clock changes that exceed a absolute 5-second variance window.
Ensure all item drops, forge evaluations, and genetic breeding mutation rolls are calculated entirely server-side, preventing client-side cheat injections.
Confirm that the Guild Trade Depot price corridors successfully lock item barter valuations between 80% and 300% of the item's baseline system value to prevent unauthorized resource transfers.
4.3 UI & Assets Production Validation Checks
Verify that all graphics assets adhere strictly to the lower-case naming namespace syntax to ensure successful automated pipeline compiling.
Confirm that the user interface layout contains zero inline gray text boxes or markdown rendering blockages, ensuring clean copy-paste functionality to destination Google Drive documentation repositories.
Assert that all localization strings map correctly across English, Czech, German, and Polish languages without throwing missing key runtime errors.

MODULE 18: LIVEOPS DEPLOYMENT PIPELINES, CLOUD INFRASTRUCTURE TOPO & EXTENDED PRODUCTION ROADMAP
1. Cloud Server Infrastructure & Network Topology Map
To sustain continuous execution monitoring for thousands of asynchronous player accounts concurrently updating up to 3 active simulation slot arrays, the cloud architecture is designed as a hybrid distributed system. It completely decouples runtime state execution from persistent data layers.
                  +-----------------------------------+                  |         Client Mobile/PC          |                  +-----------------------------------+                                    |                    HTTPS / Secure WebSocket Requests                                    v                  +-----------------------------------+                  |      Cloudflare CDN Gateway       |                  |     (DDoS Mitigation & WAF)       |                  +-----------------------------------+                                    |                                    v                  +-----------------------------------+                  |      Load Balancer Array          |                  +-----------------------------------+                                    |            +-----------------------+-----------------------+            |                                               |            v                                               v+-----------------------+                       +-----------------------+|  Stateless API Nodes  |                       |  Stateless API Nodes  ||  (ASP.NET Core / C#)  |                       |  (ASP.NET Core / C#)  |+-----------------------+                       +-----------------------+            |                                               |            +-----------------------+-----------------------+                                    |                                    v                  +-----------------------------------+                  |        Redis Cache Layer          |                  |   (Session State & Active Sync)   |                  +-----------------------------------+                                    |                         Asynchronous Batch Writes                                    v                  +-----------------------------------+                  |     PostgreSQL / Supabase         |                  |    (Primary Relational Store)     |                  +-----------------------------------+
1.1 Load Balancing and Stateless API App Gateways
Network Gateway Layer: Cloudflare CDN serves as the entry checkpoint, handling security encryption verification and DDoS attack mitigation.
Execution Infrastructure: Incoming client requests route to a Load Balancer array that distributes traffic evenly to auto-scaling API compute instances built via ASP.NET Core.
Stateless Scaling Rules: Compute nodes hold zero session memory. If traffic scales up during a seasonal event transition, new server compute instances instantiate automatically, referencing the shared Redis block memory cache for verification keys.
1.2 Transient High-Velocity Cache Specifications (Redis Layer)
Run-time resource accumulation ticks, combat health updates, and monster kill logs do not trigger immediate updates on the persistent storage database.
Data Eviction and Retention Policies: Active player data blocks are mapped into a high-speed Redis cluster cache memory segment upon client authentication.
Internal Synchronization Window: Read/write interactions track strictly inside memory memory registers. If an account drops connectivity or stays online continuously, a background system worker executes a bulk copy dump from Redis memory layers down to the core SQL tables every 5 minutes.
1.3 Asynchronous Server Workers & Cron Jobs Architecture
Top Ladders Cron Engine: Executes every 5 minutes to fetch, compute, and cache the updated global account and profession standings, rewriting a flat static data manifest block to the Redis layer for instantaneous client UI retrieval.
Guild Matchmaking Scheduler: Activates automatically every Sunday at 23:30 UTC to pair competitive groups for the weekly Guild War cycles according to the matchmaking algorithms.
World Event Cleaner: Processes the absolute damage sums of server accounts exactly at the expiration of the 24-hour World Boss timeline window, generating rewards payloads and inserting them directly into the mail tracking system rows.
2. Dynamic Client Patching Lifecycle & Hot-Fix Orchestration
To avoid forcing users to download full application packages from app stores during minor numeric updates, the engine implements a zero-downtime asset and data-patching architecture split into two operational update mechanisms.
2.1 Static System Parameter Patching (Data-Only CDNs)
Numeric data tables—such as weapon base damage curves, item drop probabilities, alchemy ingredients list recipes, or monster health values—are completely externalized from the Unity client execution compilation.
Processing Logic: Data sheets exist as raw JSON strings on an external cloud data bucket protected by global content delivery nodes.
Authentication Synchronization Handshake: When the application initializes on a device, the client transmits its local manifest version sequence token to the version api route. If a newer structural configuration file exists on the server bucket, the client automatically pulls down the updated JSON file chunk, parses the data models into the runtime ScriptableObject configurations in memory, and initializes the interface loops seamlessly.
2.2 Asset and Visual Patching via Unity Addressable Asset System
New folklore race skins, character portrait graphical layers, event field decorations, or bestiary audio tracks utilize Unity Addressable configuration grouping systems.
Memory Footprint Optimization: Visual assets are assigned explicit network addresses. The base client app bundle submitted to app marketplaces is kept below 100 megabytes.
Download Triggers: The client requests asset groups strictly on demand (such as downloading Region 02 graphical parameters exclusively when an account unlocks Level 11 milestones, or fetching event layouts only during an active event window). Downloaded files store safely to local app cache sandboxes, preventing repetitive cellular data usage.
3. Administrative Toolsets, Security Alerts & Save Reconstruction
To manage cheating attempts and handle customer support service tickets, the backend environment exposes a highly restricted administrative command layout terminal.
3.1 Automated Fraud Flag Monitoring Scripts
The server API evaluates incoming client manifest deltas against hard physical validation limits. If a transaction log breaks baseline structural possibilities, the user account is flagged instantly.
Velocity Flag 01 - Gold Modification Injections: Triggers if an account's Gold balance increases at a rate that exceeds the absolute maximum theoretical limit of three active combat units farming Region 10 bosses simultaneously with perfect quality gear over that given timeframe.
Velocity Flag 02 - Level Progress Anomalies: Triggers if character or skill level jumps do not match the geometric experience curves defined across Modules 03 and 04 relative to elapsed connection time stamps.
Automated Action Matrix: Minor flag deviations trigger immediate local memory rollback sync checks. Severe systemic structural violations (such as direct item ID fabrication injections into database slot lines) generate an immediate hard account ban flag state update and disconnect the active network socket session.
3.2 Save-State Archive Reconstruction Tooling
Customer service operators can query historical relational snapshot lines to reconstruct state timelines if database connectivity drops out or transaction processing crashes mid-transfer.
The Event Horizon Ledger: Every premium item forge sequence from Tier 7 and up, along with any Diamond transaction purchases, writes a permanent row entry to a non-volatile systemic audit tracking table before executing the shared inventory mutation.
Safe Rollback Terminals: Administrators can use this immutable ledger log to isolate an exact timestamp block and execute a full database structural recovery up to 14 calendar days retrospectively, restoring lost items directly back into the user's shared zbrojnice pool configuration.
4. Post-Launch Production Roadmap (12-Month Expansion Timeline)
4.1 Months 1 to 3: Core Infrastructure Optimization & QoL Foundations
Live Stability Tuning: Resolving database write bottlenecks during high-volume server sync events, adjusting load balancer scaling thresholds, and optimizing client-side FSM script components to minimize battery drainage on low-end mobile hardware layout models.
Interface Extensions: Implementation of advanced multi-character overview monitoring cards, advanced filtering controls inside the centralized Armory panel layout, and detailed graphical logging views tracking the specific Kills Per Hour (KPH) metrics of active grinding slots.
4.2 Months 4 to 6: Folk-Expansion Tier 01 - The Cross-Breeding Genetic Update
Lineage Fusion Matrices: Unlocks advanced Breeding Ground capabilities enabling different folklore race archetypes to cross-breed once they scale past Level 75 milestones.
Hybrid Race Paradigms: Introduction of exotic hybrid lines featuring complex inherited stat patterns and blended modifier rules (such as a Draugr-Vila cross-breed displaying Ranged Critical precision combined with localized Melee Vampirism traits, but inheriting doubled structural defensive armor scaling penalties).
4.3 Months 7 to 9: Collective Cooperative Activities - Asynchronous Guild Mega-Dungeons
Deep Labyrinth Crypts: Introduction of multi-level corporate raiding dungeons requiring guild groups to coordinate resource allocations over extended weekly cycles.
Cooperative Strike Formations: Guild members combine up to 9 distinct character profiles drawn from different user accounts into an unified tactical raid vanguard. This expeditionary army descends through dangerous multi-tier boss rooms, securing rare crafting components necessary to construct Tier 14 Transcendent equipment properties.
4.4 Months 10 to 12: End-Game System Extensions - The Transcendent Realm Ascension Path
The Soft Prestige Cycle: Characters that hit the absolute cap threshold of Level 100 can step through the Celestial Ascension Portal terminal inside the village hub boundary.
Ascension Payout Mechanics: The chosen character undergoes a complete state purification loop, resetting its progression levels back to Level 1 and stripping away all equipped items back to the general shared armory registry slots.
Permanent Village Trait Adjustments: In exchange for the progression reset, the account receives 1 Permanent Realm Ascension Token. These tokens can be allocated to upgrade structural village infrastructure systems permanently, expanding global gathering velocity metrics, unlocking exclusive item affix configurations, or permanently expanding the baseline mutation probability ratios across all future breeding cycles.

Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Balanced stats; random chance to execute high-damage area-of-effect explosive actions.
3.6 Great Kobold Overlord (Enemy ID: bos_r03_b01 - Regional Boss)
UI Lore String: The ancient, crown-wearing ruler of the deepest subterranean kingdoms. Standing three times the height of his lesser kin, he wields a massive, jewel-encrusted iron sledgehammer crafted from the first molten core deposit found beneath the Ore Crags. He commands absolute loyalty from the subterranean imp tribes and aggressively guards the primary veins from surface exploitation.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Commands massive armor rating; executes earth-shattering hammer strikes that inflict extended stun frames.
4. Region 04: Alpine Chasm Codex Entries
4.1 Mountain Eagle (Enemy ID: mob_r04_e01)
UI Lore String: Apex feathered predators nesting on the sheer vertical cliffs of the high Alps. With wingspans stretching across several meters, they possess incredible kinetic diving velocity, snatching fully equipped workers directly off mountain passes and dropping them into deep rocky chasms.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Exceptional accuracy and speed metrics; visual priority targets for ranged characters.
4.2 Crag Goat (Enemy ID: mob_r04_e02)
UI Lore String: Hardened quadrupeds with thick, reinforced skull plates and spiral horns capable of fracturing solid granite. Extremely territorial, they patrol narrow alpine ridges, charging trespassers head-on to throw them off the precipice.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: High physical block probability; attacks incorporate heavy knockback/stun potential.
4.3 Frost Lizard (Enemy ID: mob_r04_e03)
UI Lore String: Pale, cold-blooded reptiles that dwell inside perpetual ice tunnels. Their scales absorb ambient thermal energy, chilling the air around them to freezing temperatures. They freeze human boots to the ground before executing slow, calculated physical strikes.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Attacks reduce player attack speed by a fixed percentage modifier.
4.4 Rock Elemental (Enemy ID: mob_r04_e04)
UI Lore String: Living animate clusters of crystalline quartz and ancient tectonic stones bound together by primordial mountain spirits. They appear as natural scree piles until unwary gatherers step onto them, at which point they reconstruct into massive crushing shapes.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Massive flat physical armor; completely immune to critical hits and lifesteal attributes.
4.5 Alpine Wyrm (Enemy ID: mob_r04_e05 - Elite)
UI Lore String: A lesser serpentine dragon lacking wings but possessing immense muscular force and thick draconic scales. It coils around narrow chasm bridges, breathing out localized blizzards that shatter standard steel armor sets through extreme thermal shock.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Hybrid damage output; inflicts heavy physical piercing damage combined with freezing status modifiers.
4.6 Crested Tatzelwurm (Enemy ID: bos_r04_b01 - Regional Boss)
UI Lore String: A legendary alpine cryptid featuring the predatory upper torso and head of a vicious wild feline fused with the massive, armored body of a great mountain viper. It dwells within the deepest, unmapped crevices of the central chasm. Folklore claims its breath is an acidic gas that melts iron tools instantly, and its lightning-fast strikes can sever defensive shield lines before a block can be registered.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Extreme attack speed paired with high armor penetration; possesses an automated dodge matrix against ranged attacks.
5. Region 05: The Scorched Steppes Codex Entries
5.1 Field Locust (Enemy ID: mob_r05_e01)
UI Lore String: Gluttonous, armored insects that swarm across the sun-baked Pannonian plains. Arriving in vast numbers, they consume all organic matter in seconds, destroying herbalism harvesting zones and utilizing jagged mandibles to chew through leather protective gear.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Low individual health but exceptionally fast attack cycles; targets character dexterity properties.
5.2 Steppe Falcon (Enemy ID: mob_r05_e02)
UI Lore String: High-altitude avian hunters with exceptional vision parameters. They circle within the cloudless, shimmering heat distortion layers of the steppes, executing vertical stoops at speeds that create audible wind cracks, targeting the weak joints of human armor sets.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Absolute maximum base accuracy values; ignores a fixed percentage of target dodge ratings.
5.3 Blighted Vulture (Enemy ID: mob_r05_e03)
UI Lore String: Massive, disease-ridden scavengers that trail behind caravans and military detachments across the arid fields. They carry toxic pathogenetic agents on their talons, tearing open minor combat wounds to introduce rotting septic infections.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Attacks apply a heavy healing-reduction debuff, lowering food item recovery efficacy by 25%.
5.4 Dry Grass Spirit (Enemy ID: mob_r05_e04)
UI Lore String: Ethereal manifestations formed from withered flora and thermal dust devils. They drift across the steppes, sapping moisture from living tissue and creating intense localized mirages that cause combat parties to waste stamina attacking empty air.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: High natural dodge modifier; attacks inflict minor stamina/speed drain mechanics.
5.5 Sunstroke Specter (Enemy ID: mob_r05_e05 - Elite)
UI Lore String: The spiritual remains of travelers who perished from dehydration beneath the unyielding steppe sun. They appear as shimmering, translucent heat phantoms that induce severe hallucinations and thermal madness in living minds, forcing companions to turn weapons on each other.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: High critical strike damage multiplier; attacks inflict pure mental magic damage that bypasses shields.
5.6 Crimson Noon Wraith [Poludnica] (Enemy ID: bos_r05_b01 - Regional Boss)
UI Lore String: A terrifying Slavic folklore manifestation appearing exclusively as a tall, sun-bleached woman dressed in flowing white linen, wandering the fields at the exact moment of true solar noon. She catches agricultural or gathering workers who refuse to halt labor during the peak heat, challenging them to intricate, impossible riddles or executing them on the spot with a massive, rusted harvesting scythe. Her presence raises ambient temperatures to lethal thresholds, breaking down physical endurance.
Behavioral Attribute Indicator: Inflicts massive fire/physical slash hybrid damage; passive aura continuously drains character health pools every tick frame the encounter lasts.

MODULE 15: EVENT LOOP ROTATIONS, WORLD BOSS ENCOUNTERS & SEASONAL PROGRESSION ARCHITECTURES
1. Live Event Synchronization & Server Calendars
To maintain player engagement without creating progression fatigue, the game utilizes a deterministic event rotation system driven entirely by authoritative server time checks. The game client does not determine event states locally; instead, it subscribes to stateless epoch validation tokens transmitted by the database server.
1.1 Weekly Event Rotation Matrix
Every calendar month is divided into a looping sequence of four minor events. Each weekly event activates automatically on Monday at 00:00 UTC and terminates on Sunday at 23:59 UTC.
Week 1: Golden Harvest Cycle
Global Buffs: All Gathering skills (Mining, Woodcutting, Fishing, Herbalism) receive a flat +15% gathering speed reduction adjustment.
Unique Node Modification: Gathering nodes have a 5% chance to drop Event-Specific Tokens instead of raw garbage drop fillers.
Week 2: Blood Moon Vanguard
Global Buffs: Characters assigned to active Combat slots receive a flat +10% Experience Point (XP) acquisition multiplier and a +5% Lifesteal override trait.
Elite Spawn Optimization: Elite variants within all 10 regions have their baseline spawn probability doubled from standard calculation parameters.
Week 3: Master Artisan Festival
Global Buffs: Smithing, Cooking, and Alchemy professions receive a flat 20% reduction to action tick timers.
Resource Salvage Buff: Kobold and Moosleute passive item salvage properties receive a temporary +5% absolute probability boost.
Week 4: Diamond Star alignment
Global Buffs: Premium Diamond drops from standard and elite monsters are elevated from a 0.05% baseline drop chance to a 0.10% drop chance.
Forge Cost Discount: Gold requirements to merge items at the Great Forge are slashed by a flat 15% across all 14 rarity tiers.
2. World Boss Encounter Operational Matrix
World Boss events are massive, server-wide structural calculations executed over fixed 24-hour windows on the 1st and 15th days of every calendar month. The entities utilize scaling health vectors that adapt dynamically to active server population variables.
2.1 Dynamic Server Health Scaling Formula
To prevent end-game players from burning through content or locking out lower-level players, the absolute health pool of the World Boss (HP_{\text{World}}) dynamically aggregates from the total number of active accounts (A_{\text{Active}}, accounts logged in within the past 7 days) and their matching Combined Account Mastery Scores (M_{\text{Account}}).
HP_{\text{World}} = \sum_{i=1}^{A_{\text{Active}}} \left( M_{\text{Account}, i} \times 2,500 \times 1.05^{\text{Region\_Unlock\_Count}} \right)
2.2 Asynchronous Combat Resolution Loop
Entry Ticket Constraint: Every account receives exactly 3 entry attempts per World Boss event window. Each attempt allows a chosen combat character to execute attacks continuously for 5 minutes.
State Persistence: The total damage inflicted by the player’s character during the 5-minute local block is captured, signed via client-side FSM controllers, and subtracted from the global Postgres server entity row via atomic transactional updates.
Death Avoidance Override: The World Boss possesses infinite damage parameters. The player character cannot kill the boss within their isolated instance. Instead, the match ends precisely at 300 seconds, or instantly when the character's Auto-Eat food stock strikes zero.
2.3 World Event Contribution Reward Bracket
Rewards are delivered automatically via the shared Village Mailbox once the 24-hour timer expires, provided the global health pool drops to zero.
Top 1% Contribution Percentile: 1,000 Diamonds, 5x Relic-tier upgrade materials, and 1x Mythic item container.
Top 5% Contribution Percentile: 500 Diamonds, 3x Relic-tier upgrade materials, and 1x Epic item container.
Top 20% Contribution Percentile: 200 Diamonds, 1x Rare upgrade material, and 1x Ultra Rare item container.
General Participation Bracket (Dealt >0 Damage): 50 Diamonds and 50,000 flat Gold.
3. Seasonal Progression & Battle Pass Architecture
The game runs continuous 60-day themed seasons (e.g., Season of Perun's Wrath, Season of the Midsummer Vila). Seasons introduce a temporary parallel progression structure that interfaces with the permanent account state without inducing vertical stat inflation.
3.1 Non-Destructive Reset Philosophy
When a season finishes and a new one initializes, the core components of the player's account remain completely untouched to respect long-term time investments.
Permanent Assets (Never Reset): All 50 character profiles, levels, inherited genetic traits, the 50-slot housing infrastructure limits, shared gold and diamond balances, and all forged equipment up to Tier 14 Transcendent.
Volatile Seasonal Elements (Reset to Zero): Seasonal pass level standings, event-specific temporary currency tokens, and seasonal regional achievement point trackers.
3.2 The Chronicle Pass Progression Curve
The Chronicle Pass contains 50 reward steps. Advancing from Pass Level P to Level P+1 demands a flat, standardized allocation of 1,000 Seasonal Pass XP points. Seasonal Pass XP is generated from explicit daily and weekly task mandates.
Daily Challenge Block: Generates 200 Pass XP per completed objective (e.g., "Extract 500 Copper Ore", "Defeat 200 Forest Rats").
Weekly Challenge Block: Generates 1,500 Pass XP per objective (e.g., "Cook 300 Salmon Platters", "Forge 20 Iron Armor items").
3.3 Milestone Reward Allocations
The Pass is split into a Free Tier and a Premium Tier ($10.00 direct microtransaction unlock).
Level 10: Free Tier: 500,000 Gold | Premium Tier: 250 Diamonds + Exclusive Seasonal Profile Banner background.
Level 25: Free Tier: 3x Random Rare Refined Materials | Premium Tier: 1x Perfect Quality Modifier Token (Upgrades any chosen gear piece baseline quality state up one step).
Level 50 (Max Level Milestone): Free Tier: 200 Diamonds + "Season Vanguard" text title | Premium Tier: Unique Cosmetic Skin for the Draugr or Vila race lineage (0% stat modifications, visual layer adjustment only).
4. Event-Exclusive Monetization & Shop Vault Operations
To maintain strict operational health and cover server costs without crossing into pay-to-win boundaries, the Event Shop relies entirely on scarcity metrics, convenience expansions, and aesthetic customization.
4.1 The Rotating Token Market
During seasonal active cycles, actions generate Event Tokens. These tokens can be spent inside a temporary storefront that disappears at the 60-day mark.
Free Token Sinks: Players trade tokens for specialized raw material packages, tool durability recovery kits, or specific monster mastery booster scrolls.
Premium Shop Equivalents: Platting players can utilize Diamonds to purchase missing event tokens at a fixed conversion rate of 1 Diamond for 5 Event Tokens, allowing busy users to buy out pass cosmetics near the deadline.
4.2 Limited Cosmetic Vault Releases
Every season features exactly two unique character skin models tied to folklore tales. These skins are sold directly for Diamonds or fixed tier pricing and are hard-locked to that specific season calendar window, creating collectors' value through absolute scarcity.
4.3 Convenience Monetization Limitations
The engine implements hard boundaries to block economic disruption from paying players:
Equipment Blockade: Crafted gear, rarity progression tiers above Tier 3, and unique affixes cannot be bought with real currency or Diamonds. Power must be earned via active assignment slots or the server-authoritative Forge loop.
Bottleneck Restrictions: Crafting speeds, gathering cycles, and reproduction cooldown timers cannot be skipped using diamonds. Premium options only expand capacity bounds (e.g., adding automated execution slots, preservation loadouts, or offline time modifications), preserving the mathematical balance and longevity of the core progression loop.

MODULE 14: EQUIPMENT AFFIX DATABASE, CRAFTING RECEPTUARY & CONSUMABLE MATRIX
1. Item Affix Generation Engine & Stat Pools
When an equipment item rolls random secondary properties (affixes) based on its Rarity Tier constraints (Module 03), the engine selects modifiers from a dedicated pool. The values are computed dynamically based on the Region Tier (R, from 1 to 10) of the base item drop and the item's current Rarity Tier (N, from 1 to 14).
1.1 Scaling Laws for Flat Affixes
Flat affixes (such as Flat HP or Flat Armor) scale geometrically based on the intersection of item rarity and regional tiering.
\text{Value}_{\text{Flat HP}}(R, N) = \lfloor 15 \times R \times 1.22^{(N-1)} \rfloor \text{Value}_{\text{Flat Defense/Stat}}(R, N) = \lfloor 2 \times R \times 1.18^{(N-1)} \rfloor
1.2 Scaling Laws for Percentage Affixes
Percentage affixes rely purely on the Rarity Tier index (N) to prevent extreme out-of-bounds scaling in early regions, ensuring clean progression scaling.
\text{Value}_{\text{Percentage Mod}}(N) = \text{Base Value} + (\text{Growth Increment} \times (N - 1))
1.3 Complete Affix Pool Registry
Affix ID: flat_hp | Applied Slots: Helmet, Chest, Leggings, Boots, Shield, Amulet | Base Scaling: Flat HP Law.
Affix ID: flat_armor | Applied Slots: Helmet, Chest, Leggings, Boots, Shield | Base Scaling: Flat Stat Law.
Affix ID: melee_dmg_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Ring 1, Ring 2, Amulet | Base Value: 2.0% | Growth Increment: 1.5% per tier.
Affix ID: range_dmg_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Ring 1, Ring 2, Amulet | Base Value: 2.0% | Growth Increment: 1.5% per tier.
Affix ID: magic_dmg_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Ring 1, Ring 2, Amulet | Base Value: 2.0% | Growth Increment: 1.5% per tier.
Affix ID: attack_speed_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Gloves/Boots, Ring 1, Ring 2 | Base Value: 1.0% | Growth Increment: 0.5% per tier.
Affix ID: crit_chance_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Helmet, Ring 1, Ring 2 | Base Value: 0.5% | Growth Increment: 0.5% per tier.
Affix ID: crit_dmg_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Amulet, Ring 1, Ring 2 | Base Value: 5.0% | Growth Increment: 2.5% per tier.
Affix ID: lifesteal_pct | Applied Slots: Weapon, Amulet | Base Value: 0.5% | Growth Increment: 0.3% per tier.
Affix ID: armor_pen_flat | Applied Slots: Weapon, Gloves, Ring 1 | Base Scaling: Flat Stat Law.
Affix ID: dodge_chance_pct | Applied Slots: Boots, Helmet, Leggings | Base Value: 0.5% | Growth Increment: 0.4% per tier.
Affix ID: block_chance_pct | Applied Slots: Shield Only | Base Value: 1.0% | Growth Increment: 0.8% per tier.

MODULE 13: ADVANCED PROGRESSION SYSTEMS: CODEX, MONSTER MASTERY & LIFETIME ACHIEVEMENTS
1. Monster Codex & Regional Completion Engine
The Monster Codex functions as a centralized account-wide data tracking registry. It permanently logs player hunting accomplishments, drops discovered, and statistical milestones. The Codex interfaces directly with the Diamond economy and global account-wide luck systems.
1.1 Codex Tracking Schema per Entity
For every individual enemy ID across all 10 regions, the database maintains a structural JSON sub-record within the player's account profile containing:
Absolute Kill Count: Integer tracking lifetime kills.
Discovery Flags: Boolean tracking whether a specific drop from the monster's loot table has been successfully injected into the inventory at least once.
Highest Rarity Captured: Integer (1 to 14) logging the peak rarity tier ever rolled for an item drop from that specific target.
1.2 Region Completion Milestones
When a player unearths every possible drop baseline variant (at least Normal rarity) across all entities within an entire geographic region, the region state updates to Completed.
Single Monster Completion (Unlock all base drops in codex): Awards a flat 50 Diamonds and uncovers the full lore data text block in the UI.
Area Completion (All 5 standard/elite monsters in a zone fully unlocked): Awards 250 Diamonds and a unique Profile Avatar frame matching the region's aesthetic theme.
Total Region Completion (All 5 standard/elite monsters plus the Regional Boss fully completed): Grants a permanent +1% Luck modifier applied exclusively when characters execute tasks or combat loops within that specific region boundaries. It also awards 500 Diamonds.
2. Monster Mastery Tier Matrix
To incentivize long-term farming of specific nodes and maintain the economic viability of earlier game zones, every entity possesses an independent Monster Mastery Level scaled strictly by cumulative kill counts. Mastery bonuses are localized, meaning they alter combat mechanics solely against that explicit monster ID, avoiding global stat inflation.
2.1 Mastery Level Thresholds and Mathematical Progression Curve
Mastery Level 1 (Requires 100 Kills)
Localized Benefit: +2% Drop Rate chance for all items listed on this monster's standard drop table.
Mastery Level 2 (Requires 500 Kills)
Localized Benefit: +5% Gold drop scaling multiplier upon entity defeat.
Mastery Level 3 (Requires 1,000 Kills)
Localized Benefit: +5% Combat Experience Point (XP) acquisition scaling modifier.
Mastery Level 4 (Requires 5,000 Kills)
Localized Benefit: Additional +10% Drop Rate chance (Stacking additively with Tier 1 for +12% total).
Mastery Level 5 (Requires 10,000 Kills)
Localized Benefit: +1% Absolute Luck value calculation injection when evaluating loot rarity tables against this target.
Mastery Level 6 (Requires 50,000 Kills)
Localized Benefit: Additional +15% Drop Rate chance (Stacking for +27% total).
Mastery Level 7 (Requires 100,000 Kills)
Account-Wide Benefit: Unlocks the stylized Monster Portrait cosmetic option for village banners and issues a flat structural payout of 100 Diamonds.
Mastery Level 8 (Requires 1,000,000 Kills - End-Game Cap)
Localized Benefit: +2% Absolute Critical Strike Chance applied directly to player attack matrices tracking this entity.
3. Race Mastery Progression Framework
Distinct from character leveling, the account tracks a global Race Mastery Level for each of the 7 folklore lineages. Every second a character of Race X is actively assigned to an execution slot (Combat, Gathering, or Crafting), the account accumulates 1 point of Race Mastery XP for lineage X.
3.1 Race Mastery Leveling Costs
The requirement to scale Race Mastery from Level M to M+1 scales geometrically:
Mastery_XP_Required(M) = floor(3600 * 1.14^(M-1))
Level 1 to 2: 3,600 XP (1 Hour of active deployment)
Level 10 to 11: 11,707 XP
Level 25 to 26: 82,231 XP
Level 50 to 51 (Maximum Cap): 937,294 XP
3.2 High-Level Lineage Passive Advancements
Human Mastery
Level 10: Adaptability XP bonus increases from +10% to +12%.
Level 25: Unlocks a flat +5 slot expansion bonus applied to the shared Village Storage Vault.
Level 50: Adaptability modifier advances to +15% total XP generation across all profiles.
Vila Mastery
Level 10: Sylvan Precision Ranged Damage multiplier advances from +20% to +25%.
Level 25: Fragile Frame armor penalty is structurally reduced from -30% down to -20%.
Level 50: Critical Strike Chance bonus increases from +5% to +8%.
Fomóiri Mastery
Level 10: Abyssal Density flat damage reduction scales from 15 points up to 30 points.
Level 25: Sluggish Momentum spawn delay penalty is mitigated from +1.5 seconds down to +0.8 seconds.
Level 50: Flat damage reduction reaches 50 points per incoming strike frame.
Draugr Mastery
Level 10: Relentless Hunger Lifesteal percentage modifier scales from 8% up to 10%.
Level 25: Calcified Flesh healing item and food reduction penalty is cut from -50% down to -30%.
Level 50: Lifesteal capabilities scale to an absolute baseline of 12% on all melee damage calculations.
Kobold Mastery
Level 10: Subterranean Hoarder ore duplication probability scales from 15% up to 20%.
Level 25: Restricted Pack non-ore inventory slot penalty is mitigated from -50% down to -25%.
Level 50: Smithing resource salvage probability updates from 10% up to 15%.
Moosleute Mastery
Level 10: Herbalism double harvest probability factors increase from 12% up to 16%.
Level 25: Crude Handling tool durability degradation penalty drops from +25% down to +10%.
Level 50: Alchemy potion potency multiplier tracks at +15% total efficacy.
Vodník Mastery
Level 10: Active Fishing wait time reduction optimizations scale from -20% up to -25%.
Level 25: Bound to the Depths maximum offline AFK timeout constraints expand from an 8-hour cap to a 10-hour calculation cap.
Level 50: Cooking Master excellent creation event generation mechanics scale from 15% up to 22% execution probability.
